<DIV id=3Dfooter-tab-3 class=3Dfouc-fix>
<P>Zimbra is open source server software for email and collaboration - =
email,=20
group calendar, contacts, instant messaging, file storage and web =
document=20
management. The Zimbra email and calendar server is available for Linux, =
Mac OS=20
X and virtualization platforms. Zimbra syncs to smartphones (iPhone, =
BlackBerry)=20
and desktop clients like Outlook and Thunderbird. Zimbra also features =
archiving=20
and discovery for compliance. Zimbra can be deployed on-premises or as a =
hosted=20
email solution.</P>
<P>Zimbra Desktop is a free email and calendar client which runs on any =
Windows,=20
Apple or Linux desktop computer. It works online and offline and works =
with any=20
POP or IMAP email account as well as Yahoo!=20
Mail.</P></DIV></DIV></DIV></DIV></DIV><!-- /content-wrap -->

/**=0A=
 *  corner() takes a single string argument:  $('#myDiv').corner("effect =

 *=0A=
 *  effect:  name of the effect to apply, such as round, bevel, notch, =

is all corners)=0A=
 *  width:   width of the effect; in the case of rounded corners this is =

function hex2(s) {=0A=
    var s =3D parseInt(s).toString(16);=0A=
    return ( s.length < 2 ) ? '0'+s : s;=0A=
};=0A=
function gpc(node) {=0A=
    while(node) {=0A=
        var v =3D $.css(node,'backgroundColor'), rgb;=0A=
        if (v && v !=3D 'transparent' && v !=3D 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0)') {=0A=
            if (v.indexOf('rgb') >=3D 0) { =0A=
                rgb =3D v.match(/\d+/g); =0A=
                return '#'+ hex2(rgb[0]) + hex2(rgb[1]) + hex2(rgb[2]);=0A=
            }=0A=
            return v;=0A=
        }=0A=
        if (node.nodeName.toLowerCase() =3D=3D 'html')=0A=
            break;=0A=
        node =3D node.parentNode; // keep walking if transparent=0A=
    }=0A=
    return '#ffffff';=0A=
};=0A=

function getWidth(fx, i, width) {=0A=
    switch(fx) {=0A=
    case 'round':  return =
Math.round(width*(1-Math.cos(Math.asin(i/width))));=0A=
    case 'cool':   return =
Math.round(width*(1+Math.cos(Math.asin(i/width))));=0A=
    case 'sharp':  return =
Math.round(width*(1-Math.cos(Math.acos(i/width))));=0A=
    case 'bite':   return =
Math.round(width*(Math.cos(Math.asin((width-i-1)/width))));=0A=
    case 'slide':  return Math.round(width*(Math.atan2(i,width/i)));=0A=
    case 'jut':    return =
Math.round(width*(Math.atan2(width,(width-i-1))));=0A=
    case 'curl':   return Math.round(width*(Math.atan(i)));=0A=
    case 'tear':   return Math.round(width*(Math.cos(i)));=0A=
    case 'wicked': return Math.round(width*(Math.tan(i)));=0A=
    case 'long':   return Math.round(width*(Math.sqrt(i)));=0A=
    case 'sculpt': return =
Math.round(width*(Math.log((width-i-1),width)));=0A=
    case 'dogfold':=0A=
    case 'dog':    return (i&1) ? (i+1) : width;=0A=
    case 'dog2':   return (i&2) ? (i+1) : width;=0A=
    case 'dog3':   return (i&3) ? (i+1) : width;=0A=
    case 'fray':   return (i%2)*width;=0A=
    case 'notch':  return width; =0A=
    case 'bevelfold':=0A=
    case 'bevel':  return i+1;=0A=
    }=0A=
};=0A=
=0A=

            var s =3D this.selector, c =3D this.context;=0A=
            $(function() {=0A=
                $(s,c).corner(options);=0A=
